```mermaid
classDiagram
    class FVLifecycleStateMachine {
        +dict transitions
        -PackageContainerLifecycleHistoryPostgresMapping __data_store
        +__init__(application_name)
        -__validate_transition(old_state, new_state)
        +change_lifecycle(container_lifecycle, allow_duplicates) bool
        +write_batch(lifecycle_change_batch)
    }
    class PackageContainerLifecycleHistory {
        +str container_id
        +str old_state
        +str new_state
        +str reason
    }
    class PackageContainerLifecycleHistoryPostgresMapping {
        +__init__(application_name)
        +should_prevent_same_state_transition(container_id, new_state, reason) bool
        +write(container_lifecycle)
        +write_batch(lifecycle_change_batch)
    }
    class BadRequestError {
    }
    FVLifecycleStateMachine --> PackageContainerLifecycleHistoryPostgresMapping
    FVLifecycleStateMachine --> PackageContainerLifecycleHistory
    FVLifecycleStateMachine --> BadRequestError
```

## Diagram 3

```mermaid
flowchart TD
    A[Start change_lifecycle] --> B{new_state != old_state?}
    B -->|Yes| C[validate_transition]
    C -->|Valid| D[is_valid = True]
    C -->|Invalid| E[is_valid = False]
    B -->|No| F{allow_duplicates?}
    F -->|Yes| G[should_prevent_same_state_transition]
    G -->|Not Prevented| H[is_valid = True]
    G -->|Prevented| I[is_valid remains False]
    F -->|No| I
    D --> J{is_valid?}
    E --> J
    H --> J
    I --> J
    J -->|True| K[data_store.write]
    J -->|False| L[Skip write]
    K --> M[Return is_valid]
    L --> M
    M --> N[End]
```
